<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;2.02.</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Results of Operation and Financial Condition. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On February&#160;5, 2024, ON Semiconductor Corporation announced in a news release its financial performance for the fourth quarter and year ended December&#160;31, 2023 and other related material information (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Earnings Release</span></span>&#8221;). A copy of the Earnings Release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and incorporated herein by reference. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information in Item&#160;2.02 of this Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K,</span> including Exhibit 99.1, is being furnished under Item&#160;2.02 and shall not be deemed to be &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Exchange Act</span></span>&#8221;), or otherwise subject to liability under that section, nor shall such information be deemed incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, regardless of any general incorporation language in such filing, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:18pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>onsemi Reports Fourth Quarter and Full Year 2023 Earnings </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:16pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Record automotive revenue in 2023 increased 29% year-over-year </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>SCOTTSDALE, Ariz, &#150; Feb. 5, 2024 &#150;</B> <B>onsemi</B> (the &#147;Company&#148;) (Nasdaq: ON) today announced its fourth quarter
and fiscal year 2023 results with the following highlights: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="12%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Fourth quarter revenue of $2,018.1&nbsp;million </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:3pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:3pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

31.6%, respectively </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:3pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">GAAP diluted earnings per share and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted earnings per
share of $1.28 and $1.25, respectively </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:3pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:3pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

silicon carbide revenue. We continue to transform the business by building resilience into our model, enabling us to navigate uncertain market conditions and deliver more predictable and sustainable results,&#148; said Hassane <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">El-Khoury,</FONT> president and chief executive officer of onsemi. &#147;Our consistent performance has validated our long-term strategy. Looking ahead, we are driving innovation beyond silicon and silicon carbide with our
upcoming analog and mixed signal platform to further our leadership in intelligent power and sensing solutions.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:20pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Selected financial results for

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify">Diluted shares outstanding can vary as a result of, among other things, the vesting of restricted stock
units, the incremental dilutive shares from the Company&#146;s convertible senior subordinated notes, and the repurchase or the issuance of stock or convertible notes or the sale of treasury shares. In periods when the quarterly average stock price
per share exceeds $52.97 for the 0% Notes, and $103.87 for the 0.50% Notes, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted share count and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> net income per share include the anti-dilutive
impact of the Company&#146;s hedge transactions issued concurrently with the 0% Notes and the 0.50% Notes, respectively. At an average stock price per share between $52.97 and $74.34 for the 0% Notes and $103.87 and $156.78 for the 0.50% Notes, the
hedging activity offsets the potentially dilutive effect of the 0% Notes and 0.50% Notes, respectively. In periods when the quarterly average stock price exceeds $74.34 for the 0% Notes, and $156.78 for the 0.50% Notes, the dilutive impact of the
warrants issued concurrently with such notes are included in the diluted shares outstanding GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted share counts and are based on either the Company&#146;s previous quarter&#146;s average
stock price or the stock price as of the last day of the previous quarter, whichever is higher. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

special items are out of our control and could change significantly from period to period. As a result, we are not able to reasonably estimate and separately present the individual impact or probable significance of these special items, and we are
similarly unable to provide a reconciliation of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. The reconciliation that is unavailable would include a forward-looking income statement, balance sheet and statement of cash flows in
accordance with GAAP.&nbsp;For this reason, we use a projected range of the aggregate amount of special items in order to calculate our projected <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating expense outlook. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

additional way of viewing aspects of our operations that, when taken together with GAAP results and the reconciliations to corresponding GAAP financial measures that we also provide in our releases, provide a more complete understanding of factors
and trends affecting our business. Because <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are not standardized, it may not be possible to compare these financial measures with other companies&#146;

highly differentiated and innovative product portfolio, delivering intelligent power and sensing technologies that solve the world&#146;s most complex challenges and leads the way to creating a safer, cleaner, and smarter world. <B>onsemi </B>is
recognized as a Fortune 500<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> company and included in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Nasdaq-100</FONT> Index<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> and S&amp;P 500<SUP

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>NON-GAAP MEASURES </B></P>
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">To supplement the consolidated financial results prepared in accordance with GAAP, onsemi
uses <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">certain&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures,</FONT> which are adjusted from the most directly comparable GAAP measures to exclude items related to the amortization of acquisition-related intangibles, expensing of
appraised inventory fair market <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,&nbsp;inventory</FONT> valuation adjustments, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-process</FONT> research and development expenses, restructuring, asset impairments
and other, net, goodwill and intangible asset impairment charges, gains and losses on debt <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">prepayment,&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;interest</FONT> expense, actuarial (gains) losses on pension plans and other pension benefits,
third party acquisition and divestiture-related costs, tax impact of these items, and certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">other&nbsp;non-recurring&nbsp;items,</FONT> as necessary. Management does not consider the effects of these items in
evaluating the core operational activities of onsemi. Management uses <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> internally to make strategic decisions, forecast future results, and evaluate onsemi&#146;s current
performance. In addition, the Company believes that most analysts covering onsemi use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;non-GAAP</FONT> measures to evaluate onsemi&#146;s performance. Given management&#146;s and other relevant use of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures,</FONT> onsemi believes these measures are important to investors in understanding onsemi&#146;s current and future operating results as seen through the eyes of management. In addition,
management believes <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> are useful to investors in enabling them to better assess changes in onsemi&#146;s core business across different time periods. <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">These&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> are not prepared in accordance with, and should not be considered alternatives or necessarily superior to, GAAP financial data and may be different
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">from&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> used by other companies. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Because&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measures are not standardized, it may not be possible to compare these
financial measures with other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">companies&#146;&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measures, even if they have similar names. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Revenue </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> revenue allows management to evaluate, among other things, the revenue from the
Company&#146;s core businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent of special items. In addition, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> revenue is an important component of management&#146;s
internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets and forecasting future
results. Management presents this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure to enable investors and analysts to evaluate the Company&#146;s revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of operations of
onsemi&#146;s core businesses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP&nbsp;Gross</FONT> Profit and Gross Margin </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;gross</FONT> profit and gross margin allows management to evaluate, among other
things, the gross margin and gross profit of the Company&#146;s core businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;items</FONT> including, generally
speaking, amortization of acquisition-related intangibles, expensing of appraised inventory fair market <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,</FONT> impact of business wind-down and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> facility costs. In addition, it is an important component of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical
financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets, and forecasting future results. Management presents <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">this&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measure to
enable investors and analysts to evaluate our revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of revenue of onsemi&#146;s core businesses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP&nbsp;Operating</FONT> Income and&nbsp;Operating Margin </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;operating</FONT> income and operating margin allows management to evaluate,
among other things, the operating margin and operating income of the Company&#146;s core businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;items</FONT>
including, generally speaking, expensing of appraised inventory fair market <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,&nbsp;impact</FONT> of business wind-down, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> facility costs,
amortization and impairments of intangible assets, goodwill and intangible asset impairment charges, third party acquisition and divestiture related costs, restructuring charges and certain other special items as necessary. In addition, it is an
important component of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets,
obtaining targets, and forecasting future results. Management presents <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">this&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measure to enable investors and analysts to evaluate the Company&#146;s revenue generation performance
relative to the direct costs of operations of onsemi&#146;s core businesses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP&nbsp;Net</FONT>
Income Attributable to onsemi and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Diluted Earnings Per Share </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;net</FONT> income attributable to onsemi and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted earnings per share allows management to evaluate the operating results of onsemi&#146;s core
businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;items</FONT> including, generally, the amortization and impairments of intangible assets, goodwill and
intangible asset impairment charges, expensing of appraised inventory fair market <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,&nbsp;impact</FONT> of business wind down, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> facility costs,
restructuring, gains and losses on debt <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">prepayment,&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;interest</FONT> expense, actuarial (gains) losses on pension plans and other pension benefits, third party acquisition and divestiture-related
costs, discrete tax items and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">other&nbsp;non-GAAP</FONT> tax adjustments and certain other special items, as necessary. In addition, these items are important components of management&#146;s internal performance
measurement and incentive and reward process, as they are used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, setting targets, and forecasting future results. Management
presents <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measures to enable investors and analysts to understand the results of operations of onsemi&#146;s core businesses and, to the extent comparable, to compare our
results of operations on a more consistent basis against those of other companies in our industry. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">12 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>NON-GAAP MEASURES (Continued) </B></P>
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><I>Free Cash Flow </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use of free cash flow allows management to evaluate, among other things, the ability of the Company to make interest or principal payments
on its debt. Free cash flow is defined as the difference between cash flow from operating activities and capital expenditures disclosed under investing activities in the consolidated statement of cash flows. Free cash flow is not an alternative to
cash flow from operating activities as a measure of liquidity. It is an important component of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results
of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets, and forecasting future results. Management presents <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">this&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measure to enable investors and
analysts to evaluate our revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of operations of onsemi&#146;s core businesses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Diluted Share Count </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted
share count allows management to evaluate, among other things, the potential dilution due to the outstanding restricted stock units excluding the dilution from the convertible notes that is covered by hedging activity up to a certain threshold. In
periods when the quarterly average stock price per share exceeds $52.97 for the 0% Notes and $103.87 for the 0.50% Notes, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted</FONT> share count&nbsp;includes the anti-dilutive impact of
the Company&#146;s hedge transactions issued concurrently with the 0% Notes and the 0.50% Notes, respectively. At an average stock price per share between $52.97 and $74.34 for the 0% Notes and $103.87 and $156.78 for the 0.50% Notes, the hedging
activity offsets the potentially dilutive effect of the 0% Notes and the 0.50% Notes, respectively. In periods when the quarterly average stock price per share exceeds $74.34 for the 0% Notes and $156.78 for the 0.50% Notes, the dilutive impact of
the warrants issued concurrently with such notes are included in the diluted shares outstanding. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">13 </P>

</DIV></Center>
